-- Table: bokemon_info
CREATE TABLE bokemon_info (bid INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT NOT NULL, bname TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE, "desc" TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE, population INTEGER NOT NULL, type TEXT NOT NULL, rid INTEGER REFERENCES region (rid) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE NOT NULL);

CREATE TABLE friends (uid INTEGER NOT NULL REFERENCES user (uid) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE, fid INTEGER NOT NULL REFERENCES user (uid) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE);
